<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><span style="font-size: 10pt"><b>Item 2.02</b></span> <span style="font-size: 10pt"><b>Results of Operations and Financial Condition.</b></span></p>


<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">On March 24, 2023, IT Tech Packaging, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;)
issued a press release announcing its financial results and operational results for the fourth quarter and fiscal year ended December
31, 2022. A copy of the press release making the announcement is attached as Exhibit 99.1 to this Current Report on Form 8-K and is incorporated
herein by reference.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<DESCRIPTION>PRESS RELEASE DATED MARCH 24, 2023, ANNOUNCING FINANCIAL RESULTS AND OPERATIONAL RESULTS OF THE COMPANY FOR THE FOURTH QUARTER AND FISCAL YEAR ENDED DECEMBER 31, 2022
<TEXT>
<HTML>
<HEAD>
     <TITLE></TITLE>
</HEAD>
<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="text-align: right; margin: 0"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0; text-align: right">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center; background-color: white"><B>IT Tech Packaging,
Inc. Announces Fourth Quarter and Fiscal Year 2022 Financial Results</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center; background-color: white"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">BAODING,&nbsp;China,&nbsp;March 24, 2023&nbsp;/PRNewswire/
--&nbsp;IT Tech Packaging, Inc. (NYSE American: ITP) (&ldquo;IT Tech Packaging&rdquo; or the &ldquo;Company&rdquo;), a leading manufacturer
and distributor of diversified paper products in&nbsp;North China, today announced its unaudited financial results for the fourth&nbsp;quarter&nbsp;and
audited financial results for the fiscal year&nbsp;ended&nbsp;December 31, 2022.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Mr. Zhenyong Liu, Chairman and Chief Executive
Officer of the Company, commented, &ldquo;In fiscal year 2022, our business execution was reflected as we generated approximately $100.35
million in revenue and approximately $4.75 million in gross profit. With the domestic business and markets resumption in an orderly manner
as the pandemic is gradually under control in China, we expect that the market demand for our products will recover gradually. &ldquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>Fourth Quarter 2022 Financial Results</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; background-color: white"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol; font-size: 10pt">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD>Revenue decreased by 52.6% to&nbsp;approximately $21.37 million, primarily attributable to an decrease in sales volume of all categories
of products and decrease in ASP of CMP.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; background-color: white"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol; font-size: 10pt">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD>Gross profit decreased by 76.3% to&nbsp;approximately $1.03 million. Total gross margin decreased by 4.8 percentage point to 4.8%.&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; background-color: white"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol; font-size: 10pt">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD>Loss from operations was&nbsp;approximately $0.49 million, compared to operation income of&nbsp;approximately $1.95 million&nbsp;for
the same period of last year.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; background-color: white"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol; font-size: 10pt">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD>Net loss was&nbsp;approximately $11.91 million, or loss of $1.19&nbsp;per basic and diluted share, compared to net income of&nbsp;approximately
$4.16 million, or earnings of&nbsp;$0.45&nbsp;per basic and diluted share, for the same period of last year.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; background-color: white"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><I>Revenue</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">For the fourth quarter of 2022, total revenue
decreased by&nbsp;approximately $23.7 million, or 52.6%, to&nbsp;approximately $21.4 million&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately $45.0 million&nbsp;for
the same period of last year. The decrease in total revenue was mainly due to the decrease in sales volume of CMP, offset printing paper
and tissue paper products and the decrease in ASP of CMP and offset printing paper.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">The following table summarizes revenue, volume
and ASP by product for the fourth quarter of 2022 and 2021, respectively:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Revenue from CMP, including both regular CMP
and light-Weight CMP, decreased by&nbsp;$18.6 million, or 46.9%, to&nbsp;approximately $21.1 million&nbsp;and accounted for 98.5 % of
total revenue for the fourth quarter of 2022, compared to&nbsp;approximately $39.7 million, or 88.0% of total revenue, for the same period
of last year. The Company sold 51,306 tonnes of CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$410/tonne in the fourth quarter of 2022, compared to 69,953 tonnes
at an ASP of&nbsp;$567/tonne in the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Of the total CMP sales, revenue from regular
CMP decreased by&nbsp;approximately $15.4 million, or 47.1%, to&nbsp;approximately $17.3 million, resulting from sales of 41,941 tonnes
at an ASP of&nbsp;$412/tonne, during the fourth quarter of 2022, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately$32.7 million, resulting from
sales of 57,410 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$569/tonne, for the same period of last year. Revenue from light-weight CMP decreased by&nbsp;approximately
$3.2 million, or 46.1%, to&nbsp;approximately $3.8 million, resulting from sales of 9,365 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$402/tonne for the
fourth quarter of 2022, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately $7.0 million, resulting from sales of 12,543 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$558/tonne
for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Revenue from offset printing paper was $nil
for the three months ended December 31, 2022, due to COVID-19, offset printing paper was suspended in 2022. Revenue from offset printing
paper was &nbsp;approximately $3.0 million&nbsp;for the fourth quarter of 2021, with 3,911 tonnes sold at an ASP of&nbsp;$759/tonne.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Revenue from tissue paper products decreased
by&nbsp;$2.0 million, or 88.9%, to&nbsp;approximately $0.3 million, resulting from sales of 234 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$1,083/tonne,
for the fourth quarter of 2022, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately$2.3million, resulting from sales of 2,292 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$994/tonne
for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Revenue from face masks decreased by&nbsp;$89,508,
or 61.2%, to&nbsp;approximately $56,774&nbsp;&nbsp;for the fourth quarter ended&nbsp;December 31, 2022, from $146,282 for the same period
of 2021. The Company sold 1,330 thousand pieces of face masks for the fourth quarter ended&nbsp;December 31, 2022, compared to 3,014 thousand
pieces of face masks for the same period of 2021.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 2; Options: NewSection; Value: 2 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->2<!-- Field: /Sequence --></P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><I>Gross Profit and Gross Margin</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Total cost of sales decreased by&nbsp;$20.3
million, or 49.9%, to&nbsp;approximately $20.4 million&nbsp;for the fourth quarter of 2022 from&nbsp;approximately $40.7 million&nbsp;for
the same period of last year. For paper products, overall cost of sales per tonne was&nbsp;$394&nbsp;for the fourth quarter of 2022, compared
to&nbsp;$533&nbsp;for the same period of last year. The decrease in overall cost of sales was mainly due to the decrease in sales volume
of CMP and offset printing paper and decrease of material costs of CMP in the fourth quarter of 2022.&nbsp; Costs of sales per tonne for
regular CMP, light-weight CMP, offset printing paper, and tissue paper products were&nbsp;$378,&nbsp;$361,&nbsp;$nil and&nbsp;$4,494,
respectively, for the fourth quarter of 2022, compared to&nbsp;&nbsp;$514,&nbsp;$490,&nbsp;$596, and&nbsp;$1,132, respectively, for the
same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Total gross profit was&nbsp;approximately
$1.0 million&nbsp;for the fourth quarter of 2022, compare to the gross profit of&nbsp;approximately$4.3 million&nbsp;for the same period
of last year as a result of factors described above. Overall gross margin was 4.8% for the fourth quarter of 2022, compared to 9.6% for
the same period of last year. Gross profit (loss) margins for regular CMP, light-weight CMP, offset printing paper, tissue paper products
and face mask products were 8.3%, 10.3%, n/a, -315.2% and 27.5%, respectively, for the fourth quarter of 2022, compared to 9.6%, 12.2%,
21.5%, -13.9% and 25.2%, respectively, for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><I>Selling, General and Administrative Expenses</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Selling, general and administrative expenses
(&ldquo;SG&amp;A&rdquo;) decreased by&nbsp;$0.9million, or 36.4%, to&nbsp;approximately $1.5 million&nbsp;for the fourth quarter of 2022
from&nbsp;approximately$2.4 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><I>Income (Loss) from Operations</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Loss from operations was&nbsp;approximately
$0.5million&nbsp;for the fourth quarter of 2022, a decrease of $2.4 million, or 125.2%, from income from operations of&nbsp;approximately
$2.0 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year. Operating loss margin was -2.3% for the fourth quarter of 2022, compared to operating
margin of 4.3% for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><I>Net Income (Loss)</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Net loss was&nbsp;approximately $11.9 million,
or&nbsp;$1.19&nbsp;loss per basic and diluted share for the fourth quarter of 2022, representing a decrease of $16.1 million, or 386.6%,
from net income of&nbsp;approximately $4.2 million, or&nbsp;$0.45 earnings&nbsp;per basic and diluted share, for the same period of last
year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><I>EBITDA</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">EBITDA was&nbsp;approximately $3.8 million&nbsp;for
the fourth quarter of 2022, compared to&nbsp;approximately $8.7 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Note 1: Non-GAAP Financial Measures</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">In addition to our U.S. GAAP results, this
press release includes a discussion of EBITDA, a non-GAAP financial measure as defined by the Securities and Exchange Commission (&ldquo;SEC&rdquo;).
The Company defines EBITDA as net income before interest, income taxes, depreciation and amortization. EBITDA is a key measure used by
management to evaluate our results and make strategic decisions. Management believes this measure is useful to investors because it is
an indicator of operational performance. Because not all companies use identical calculations, the Company&rsquo;s presentation of EBITDA may
not be comparable to similarly titled measures of other companies, and should not be viewed as an alternative to measures of financial
performance or changes in cash flows calculated in accordance with the U.S. GAAP.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"></P>

</TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><I>Revenue</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">For the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2022, total
revenue decreased by&nbsp;$60.5 million, or 37.6%, to&nbsp;approximately $100.4 million&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately$160.9 million&nbsp;for
2021. The decrease in total revenue was mainly due to the decrease in sales volume of CMP, offset printing paper and tissue paper and
the decrease in ASP of CMP.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"></P>

    <TD STYLE="width: 1%; text-align: left">&nbsp;</TD><TD STYLE="width: 9%; text-align: right">46</TD><TD STYLE="width: 1%; text-align: left">&nbsp;</TD></TR>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Revenue from CMP, including both regular CMP
and light-Weight CMP decreased by&nbsp;$35.8 million, or 26.6%, to&nbsp;approximately $98.7 million, and accounted for 98.4% of total
revenue for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2022, compared to&nbsp;&nbsp;approximately$134.5 million, or 83.6% of total revenue for 2021.
The Company sold 218,331tonnes of CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$452/tonne in the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2022, compared to 259,691tonnes
at an ASP of&nbsp;$518/tonne in 2021.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Of the total CMP sales, revenue from regular
CMP decreased by&nbsp;$28.8 million, or 25.9%, to&nbsp;approximately $82.3 million, resulting from sales of 180,977 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$455/tonne
during the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2022, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately$111.1 million, resulting from sales of 213,490
tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$520/tonne for 2021. Revenue from light-weight CMP decreased by&nbsp;$7.0 million, or 29.9%, to&nbsp;approximately$16.4
million, resulting from sales of 37,354 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$440/tonne for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2022, compared to revenue
of&nbsp;approximately$23.4million, resulting from sales of 46,201tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$507/tonne for 2021.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Revenue from offset printing paper was $nil
for the year ended December 31, 2022 compared to the revenue of $17.1 for the year ended December 31, 2021. Due to COVID-19, our paper
production was restricted and production of offset printing paper was suspended in 2022.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Revenue from tissue paper products decreased
by&nbsp;$7.4 million, or 84.5%, to&nbsp;approximately $1.4 million, resulting from sales of 1,273 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$1,065/tonne,
for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2022, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately $8.8 million, resulting from sales of 8,255 tonnes
at an ASP of&nbsp;$1,062/tonne for 2021.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Revenue from face masks decreased by&nbsp;$0.3
million, or 52.1%, to&nbsp;approximately $0.3 million&nbsp;for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2022, from approximately $0.5 million
for 2021. The Company sold 5,625 thousand pieces of face masks for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2022, compared to 12,664 thousand
pieces of face masks for 2021.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><I>Gross Profit and Gross Margin</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Total cost of sales decreased by $54.2 million,
or 36.1%, to&nbsp;approximately $95.6 million&nbsp;for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2022&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately $149.9 million&nbsp;for
2021. The decrease in overall cost of sales was mainly due to the decreased sales volume of CMP and offset printing paper and decreased
material costs of CMP in the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2022.&nbsp; Costs of sales per tonne for regular CMP, light-weight CMP, offset
printing paper, tissue paper products were,&nbsp;$421,&nbsp;$398,&nbsp;$nil, and&nbsp;$3,370, respectively, for the year ended&nbsp;December
31, 2022&nbsp;compared to&nbsp;$487,&nbsp;$463,&nbsp;$570, and&nbsp;$1,214, respectively, for 2021.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-right: 0; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Total gross profit decreased by&nbsp;$6.3
million, or 56.9%, to&nbsp;approximately $4.8 million&nbsp;for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2022&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately $11.0
million&nbsp;for 2021. Overall gross margin decreased by 2.2 percentage points to 4.7% for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2022&nbsp;from
6.9% for 2021. Gross margins for regular CMP, light-weight CMP, offset printing paper, tissue paper products and face mask products were
7.4%, 9.4%, nil, -216.3% and 26.1%, respectively, for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2022, compared to 6.3%, 8.7%, 18.2%, 14.3% and
19.2%, respectively, for 2021.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><I>Selling, General and Administrative Expenses</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">SG&amp;A expenses increased by&nbsp;$0.5 million,
or 5.24%, to&nbsp;approximately $10.1 million&nbsp;for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2022&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately $9.6 million&nbsp;for
2021. As a percentage of total revenue, SG&amp;A expenses was 10.0% for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2022, compared to 5.9% for 2021.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><I>Income (Loss) from Operations</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Loss from operations decreased by&nbsp;$6.8
million, or 463.5% to&nbsp;approximately $5.3 million&nbsp;for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2022&nbsp;from income from operations
of&nbsp;approximately $1.5 million&nbsp;for 2021. Operating loss margin was -5.3% for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2022, compared
to operating margin of 0.9% for 2021.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><I>Net Income (Loss)</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><I>&nbsp;</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Net loss decreased by&nbsp;$17.5 million,
or 1930.0%, to&nbsp;approximately $16.6 million, or losses per basic and diluted share of&nbsp;$1.66, for the year ended&nbsp;December
31, 2022, compared to net income of&nbsp;approximately $0.9 million, or earnings per basic and diluted share of&nbsp;$0.10 for 2021.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><I>EBITDA</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><I>&nbsp;</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">EBITDA decreased by&nbsp;$12.0 million, or
52.2%, to&nbsp;approximately $11.0 million&nbsp;for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2022&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately $22.9 million&nbsp;for
2021.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Note 1: Non-GAAP Financial Measures</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">In addition to our U.S. GAAP results, this
press release includes a discussion of EBITDA, a non-GAAP financial measure as defined by the Securities and Exchange Commission (&ldquo;SEC&rdquo;).
The Company defines EBITDA as net income before interest, income taxes, depreciation and amortization. EBITDA is a key measure used by
management to evaluate our results and make strategic decisions. Management believes this measure is useful to investors because it is
an indicator of operational performance. Because not all companies use identical calculations, the Company&rsquo;s presentation of EBITDA may
not be comparable to similarly titled measures of other companies, and should not be viewed as an alternative to measures of financial
performance or changes in cash flows calculated in accordance with the U.S. GAAP.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>Cash, Liquidity and Financial Position</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">As of&nbsp;December 31, 2022, the Company
had cash and bank balances, short-term debt (including bank loans, current portion of long-term loans from credit union and related party
loans), and long-term debt (including loan from credit union) of&nbsp;approximately $9.5&nbsp;million,&nbsp;$11.2&nbsp;million and&nbsp;$4.2&nbsp;million,
respectively, compared to&nbsp;&nbsp;approximately $11.2&nbsp;million,&nbsp;$13.5&nbsp;million and&nbsp;$3.0&nbsp;million, respectively,
at the end of 2021.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Net accounts receivable was&nbsp;approximately
$0.9&nbsp;million as of&nbsp;December 31, 2022, compared to&nbsp;&nbsp;approximately $4.9 million&nbsp;as of&nbsp;December 31, 2021. Net
inventory was&nbsp;approximately $2.9&nbsp;million as of&nbsp;December 31, 2022, compared to&nbsp;approximately $5.8 million&nbsp;at the
end of 2021. As of&nbsp;December 31, 2022, the Company had current assets of&nbsp;approximately $47.2&nbsp;million and current liabilities
of&nbsp;approximately $17.6&nbsp;million, resulting in a working capital of&nbsp;approximately $29.6&nbsp;million. This was compared to
current assets of&nbsp;approximately $55.5&nbsp;million and current liabilities of&nbsp;approximately $20.4 million, resulting in a working
capital of&nbsp;approximately $35.1&nbsp;million at the end of 2021.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Net Cash provided by operating activities
was&nbsp;approximately $10.7 million&nbsp;for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2022, compared to net cash used in operating activities
of approximately $2.4 million&nbsp;for 2021. Net cash used in investing activities was&nbsp;approximately $10.9 million&nbsp;for the year
ended&nbsp;December 31, 2022, compared to&nbsp;approximately $25.1 million&nbsp;for 2021. Net cash used in financing activities was&nbsp;approximately
$0.9 million&nbsp;for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2022, compared to net cash provided by financing activities of&nbsp;approximately
$34.2 million&nbsp;for 2021.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>About IT Tech Packaging, Inc.</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Founded in 1996, IT Tech Packaging, Inc. is
a leading manufacturer and distributor of diversified paper products and single-use face masks in&nbsp;North China. Using recycled paper
as its primary raw material (with the exception of its tissue paper products), ITP produces and distributes three categories of paper
products: corrugating medium paper, offset printing paper and tissue paper products. With production based in Baoding and Xingtai in&nbsp;North
China&rsquo;s&nbsp;Hebei Province, ITP is located strategically close to the&nbsp;Beijing&nbsp;and&nbsp;Tianjin&nbsp;region, home to a growing
base of industrial and manufacturing activities and one of the largest markets for paper products consumption in the country. ITP has
been listed on the NYSE American since&nbsp;December 2009. For more information, please visit:&nbsp;https://www.itpackaging.cn/.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>
